<Text>Westside Pizza. We went to pay a visit to the new pizzaria in town. About two months open at this time. Located next door from Taco Bell. Clean and bright facility. They pride themselves on all fresh ingredients. As is the main emphasis on todays eateries these days. The operation was chaotic. All employees, including manager are quite young. All appeared to be upbeat even though they were frazzled and behind schedule. Aside from a hectic operation we waited for 45 min. (As a dine in customer). When I decided I should ask what the status of our order. Was told they could not find our order. Manager promptly refunded our money and gave out courtesy tickets for additional pizzas. As far as the food? I can describe as little Caesars pizza sold at round table pizza prices. The facility does have a small banquet area with about five arcade games. I dont like to write a negative review, especially toward a new bussiness. But times are tough and money is tight for everyone.  Would i return visit Westside pizza? < text>
Was looking for a place to buy quality motorcycle gear close to home and at a reasonable price.  This is where I was recommended to go and they were right!  Sales staff is very helpful, even with someone 100% new to riding.  I went initially for a helmet.  Saleswoman was very knowledgeable and helpful.  Encouraged me to try lots of different ones on and wear them for 5 minutes or so to see how they felt.  I was able to find the perfect one for my head but it did take trying on more than a couple.  They are more than willing to order whatever you want in the color you want if they don't have it in stock and they do have a LOT!  I have already gone back for a couple of additional items and have a leather jacket on order, picking up two days after ordering!  Prices are much better than other places I went.  I will be making this my go to place for motorcycle gear!</text>

<Review>This would've gotten 4 stars but I'm a bit disappointed that even though I ordered a 2 donuts w a drink I wasn't even offered the special donut cup w my drink :/ I didn't even know until I saw other customers w it. Pretty sad.

Earl gray blueberry mochi donut:
Pretty good but I don't necessarily taste the earl grey. It tastes more like blueberry w a slight herbal tea tartness. Also the donuts aren't as oily tasting as fill and still taste pretty good refrigerated.

Ube mochi donut:
Has that coconut vanilla mild taro flavor rather than a rich and creamy ube. It's good but not what I expected.

Ube hayala milk tea w dragon boba:
The boba is actually pretty good. No weird raisin flavor from the brown sugar. The drink is alright; it's a bit on the sweet side. It's more like a taro milk tea rather than ube hayala.

< review>
About 2 years ago, I needed a large storage unit for my belongings. Heritage Storage  was the only storage place at that time with the larger units.  At first I thought they were a bit expensive, I had not had this large of a unit before. I left and looked around some more. I did a comparison to Modesto's storages with same large unit.  To my suprise, Heritage was less expensive than Modesto Storages.! And it was close to my home.
I am so happy that I came here for  many reasons.  I like the fact it is gated with a security code. (and if the owners feel there is a safety or security issue, they will change the structure of the code. Which I think is absolutely responsible and smart!)  Heritage is also a very clean business, they are  open 24/7,  and have a great staff. They are not intimidating, they are caring and actually have helped with understanding a financial situation I had.  Vicki who is a wonderful, caring person, helped me by calling me on occasions, and emailing me,  gently reminding me of   due dates and the latest I could pay without compiling late fees or lien fees.I totally appreciated the fact that she  cares!
I would definitely recommend this storage unit for any size storage you need.  The accommodations, and extras and the staff are something you just don't experience with other storage businesses.

Thank you for your great service<//review>

<Review>I've visited this business twice. The first time went fine. I brought in my cat, Oliver, because a kitten we were taking care of gave him fleas. The kitten was young enough and small enough I felt confident I could bathe her myself. The pricing was described vaguely. Base price was $50 but depending how difficult he was could make the price jump (??) and aside from a weird comment at pick up, I was satisfied that Oliver was clean and flea free.

This second and last visit was much worse. We ended up keeping that kitten, and she is now about a year old. I noticed Oliver had dandruff and after looking closer found a single flea. I figured probably more, and asked my roommate to take the both of them for flea baths.  I thought, might as well pay the money and make it easier on me instead of bathing two cats and maybe not getting it all in one go. While the cats were getting baths, I flea bombed the apartment. When my roommate went to go pick up the cats, the employee mentioned that if the cats still have fleas they do re-baths for $20 if we come back within the next 12 or so days. I thought that was odd since that wasn't mentioned the first time I picked up just Oliver. They also charged me $55 for Oliver the first time, and $45 per cat this time... Very next day we found two fleas on Oliver in the morning, and the kittens itching has only gotten worse. (Harder to check her for visual confirmation since most of her fur is black). It seems like they didn't do a very thorough job, knew that, and mentioned that $20 dollar 'deal'. I'm not going to bother going back. Why pay another $40 for sub par services? On my next break from work, I'm going to have to bathe both of them, bomb my apartment again, and then I'm just going to go get Advantage from a nearby petco. < Review>
I have had my two Soft Coated Wheaton Terriers groomed for many years now - and I know what to look for in terms of a groomer's skills, attention to detail, understanding and patience.  I am also very particular about how they are cut as its not the traditional look....from day 1 their service and care has been exemplary.  When I moved to San Diego I wished I could have found a hairdresser for myself so easily!

I should also mention that grooming dogs and cats is far from an easy job - you need to train your animals to except grooming from an early age....often burns and cuts occur because the animal is untrained, scared or its coat or nails are a mess because the owner left it too long and now it's just a painful event.  If you have concerns then asked to be with your pet for the first time - be responsible if you have been irresponsible!  I am fed up seeing these types of claims of abuse when I have personally seen the care given to all the animals here - and in 12  random visits all I have seen is a calm working environment with manageable pets!

I have been to this little place a couple times over the years.  The food is good but not the best in town.  Don't order any white wine.  I ordered their white wine and they offered two kinds, both were Woodride, which is very cheap and do not recommend anyone.  The food could be presented better on the plates in a more appealing way. < Date>

<UserId.>116053515487216770690</UserId.><text>This restaurant's tag line, "reminiscent of things Thai," describes its food very well. Most menu items are recognizable Thai restaurant classics - curries, noodles, seafood dishes - all done well; also listed are also a number of authentic but offbeat-Thai and fusion dishes.

Some of my favorite mains: spicy noodles with tofu; duck curry; pumpkin curry with pork; shrimp paste fried rice; favorite starters: nam sod, larb, egg rolls, calamari. The most unique dish is the country curry: a yellow curry made with no coconut milk and added spices such as a large sprig of juniper - extremely spicy and flavorful!

One good measure of a restaurant is how well it does on the simplest dishes. Let's take the common, humble praram rong song: a protein floating in peanut sauce, usually served on a bed of spinach. At Zenyai this dish uses wilted spinach leaves, not quite raw but still with plenty of structure; the peanut sauce is spicy, savory, and not too sweet, and although there's a gracious amount, there's not enough sauce to drown the spinach. Every bite of praram is enjoyable and the meat is clearly cooked in the sauce, not added at the last minute.

If you want creative, healthy, fresh, original Thai, Zenyai is your choice. If you want sugar- and fish-sauce heavy, restaurant-style classics, you would be better served by one of the other Thai options in town.<//text></record></dataset><record>

My husband and I and our pup lived here, all of 13 days. We moved in mid-June 18 and moved out by the end of the month!

We wanted to live in a cheaper area so we made the move from Sunnyvale to Milpitas. The rent was at a great (for the bay area) price point and the community was beautiful.
The community is still relatively new and had a modern/ upscale feel. We chose the 701 sq ft one bedroom with a beautiful pool view. The common areas and pool were well maintained. I loved the little conference areas and the pet walk!

We had a temp leaser at the time who didn‚Äôt really know the community but when Yolonda Longmire came back, from lunch, she was very friendly and helpful. She made the application and move-in process quick and easy!

The apartment was a little tight but we managed to fit and organize everything nicely. We had moved in and unpacked in 2 days (I hate clutter). I noticed a small bug in the kitchen cabinet while unpacking but assumed it was due to the apartment being vacant, killed it and continued unpacking. Immediately I noticed stains on the carpet and the bathroom and kitchen floor were dirty. When we walked barefoot our feet turned black. I informed Yolonda and this was easily remedied by the maintenance team. They came and re-cleaned and all was well or so we thought. On night three the nightmare began!

We had moved into an apartment that was infested with roaches! I say infested because that ‚Äúharmless bug‚Äù I saw on night one was a baby roach!! Which was confirmed when the countless other baby roaches and full-on adult roaches started coming out of every nook and cranny! We immediately began to self treat and put in a Service Request for Pest Control. These pests were everywhere! I was afraid to cook to shower to sleep! They would run across the kitchen walls as I go to turn the light on. I found them in my clothing, in the closet and under our bed. We immediately talked to management because we knew we did not have roaches at our previous apartment. Long story short, they scheduled Pest Control to come ‚Äúcheck‚Äù our apartment. After further investigation, it was discovered that the first floor unit had put in a request to have that apartment treated for roaches. It was treated and they moved out but the roaches had made their way upstairs to the second floor. But they never requested treatment and we just so happened to move in on top of them!!

Kristy and Yolonda worked diligently to schedule treatment of our unit but I was completely freaked out and uncomfortable living there. <text>I currently live in Ilara and have waited to write a review until now so I could really get a feel for the place.

Move in: The staff here are very nice, both office and maintenance staff, we had to wait awhile with some minor repairs when we moved into our unit that weren't fixed when we moved in but they were resolved without too much issue, we had our sink blow out in week 2 and our screen in our living room needed to be replaced, not too big of a deal the maintenance staff are great. We did get charged $100 for a late fee on our first months rent which was fine because we were a day late, the only problem with that was we never were really told how to pay our rent I guess you are just expected to figure it out online, oh and if you pay online you get hit with HUGE charges from the payment company, no joke, it's nuts.

Apartment: We really like the apartment honestly it's very modern and comfortable, there's lots of plugs for electronics and modern cable wiring for high speed internet which is a huge plus for young people. the bathroom is big in our unit but our bedroom is small, I honestly wish the bathroom was smaller and the bedroom bigger all of our bedroom furniture barely fits so you can walk around. Otherwise everything is great, we really like the place.

Security/Parking Garage: Here is the big issue with the complex that needs to be said, THE PARKING GARAGE GATE IS ALWAYS BROKEN! which means random people can bypass the whole stupid security system and go into the building and just walk around or vandalize peoples vehicles!!! Literally I've seen the gate wide open for strangers probably 30% of the time I've been here and it's honestly alarming, there is only passkey security on the first floor which makes sense....if the gate works or if people don't let strangers follow them through the gate. My girlfriend and I have had 4 packages stolen off our porch in the past week alone and there is 0 security once you get past the first floor. We are supposed to be getting parcel lockers at some point but as it stands we have lost $300 in products due to lack of security in the building and luckily our cars have been okay at least. This is the real reason for my poor review and the low rating does not go towards the staff here at all, literally the security needs to be increased here because it's just poor right now as it stands. There also seems so be a perpetual problem with people littering in the stairwells and parking garages which is totally a problem with the people living here and not an issue with the building or the staff here, the people here are just too lazy to throw their trash in the chutes or in trash cans.

I would absolutely bump this rating up if the package issue was solved, hopefully the new lockers fix this problem but the delivery drivers don‚Äôt always follow the instructions you setup for delivery.

***Updated Review***

On my updated review I can only give Ilara a 4 star review. The staff here are great, but I've grown to notice they need a lot more security in this building, I felt unsafe after our packages were being stolen off our porch (and they still are if they don't go to the leasing office) that we bought a Nest security system. There needs to be a huge upgrade in the security here including the parking garage, we have had way too many things stolen off our porch, and it doesn't make us feel comfortable at all! We are talking about moving out soon to get away from the commercialized buildings because this one has basic security and is a target for theft. I have no way of knowing if it‚Äôs our neighbors taking things off our porch or if it‚Äôs someone getting into the building.
